# The galaxy

| [This article covers the Canon version of this subject.](/wiki/The_galaxy "This article covers the Canon version of this subject.") |  | [Click here for Wookieepedia's article on the Legends version of this subject.](/wiki/The_galaxy/Legends "Click here for Wookieepedia's article on the Legends version of this subject.") |  |

[![OnACanonArticle](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Canon "Canon")[![GoToLegends](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/The_galaxy/Legends "The galaxy/Legends")

This article is about **the galaxy**. You may be looking for **the magazine [*Star Wars Galaxy*](/wiki/Star_Wars_Galaxy_Magazine "Star Wars Galaxy Magazine") or other [galaxies](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy")**.

[![The Galaxy - TROS Visual Dictionary](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/The_Galaxy_-_TROS_Visual_Dictionary.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/499?cb=20250802011341)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/The_Galaxy_-_TROS_Visual_Dictionary.png/revision/latest?cb=20250802011341 "The Galaxy - TROS Visual Dictionary")

## The galaxy

## Astrographical information

### Total stars

Over 400 billion (estimated)[[1]](#cite_note-VE-1)

### Total star systems

180 billion[[2]](#cite_note-BMF_34-2)

* 3.2 billion habitable[[1]](#cite_note-VE-1) (ca. 1 billion inhabited)[[3]](#cite_note-SG-3)

### Size

* Around 120,000 [light-years](/wiki/Light-year "Light-year")[[4]](#cite_note-Altaya-4)
  + Approximately 105,000 light-years on the y-axis[[5]](#cite_note-CE25_light-year_note-5)
  + Approximately 115,000 light-years on the x-axis[[5]](#cite_note-CE25_light-year_note-5)

### Galactic arms

[Tingel Arm](/wiki/Tingel_Arm "Tingel Arm")[[6]](#cite_note-Catalyst-6)

### Sentient species

Millions of [sentient](/wiki/Sentience "Sentience") [species](/wiki/Species "Species")[[13]](#cite_note-TSWB-13)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Galaxy)

:   "*You have a powerful imagination. When you want to, you see grand adventures, even in a rotten galaxy like this. Remember: your focus determines your reality. You have vision. Embrace it. Make your life the one you wanna live.*"
:   ―[Jod Na Nawood](/wiki/Jod_Na_Nawood "Jod Na Nawood"), to [Wim](/wiki/Wim "Wim")[[14]](#cite_note-SC5-14)

**The galaxy**, as it was commonly referred to, was one of trillions of [galaxies](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") in the [observable universe](/wiki/Universe "Universe"). The galaxy was a vast composite of over 400 billion estimated [stars](/wiki/Star "Star") and over 3.2 billion habitable [systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") orbiting around a supermassive [black hole](/wiki/Black_hole "Black hole") known as the [Galactic Centre](/wiki/Galactic_Centre "Galactic Centre"), which existed at the [heart](/wiki/Heart "Heart") of the galaxy. The four galactic arms rotated around this black hole across a diameter of around 120,000 [light-years](/wiki/Light-year "Light-year"). It was home to countless [sentient](/wiki/Sentience "Sentience") [species](/wiki/Species "Species") and star systems.

The galaxy would serve as the setting for society, trade, [politics](/wiki/Politics "Politics"), and war throughout [galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history"). In historical memory, the galaxy would see the successive eras of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), among others, and was home to the [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") sects such as the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") and [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") and numerous cultural groups such as the [Mandalorians](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian").

## Astrography[]

### Overview[]

:   "*...be transported from the Outer Rim to as far away as the Core Worlds. However there are several other regions within our galaxy. They are the Mid Rim...The Expansion Region, the Inner Rim, the Colonies, Core, and Deep Core.*"
:   ―A [protocol droid teacher](/wiki/Unidentified_protocol_droid_teacher "Unidentified protocol droid teacher") to her students[[15]](#cite_note-Chapter_12-15)

 [![The galaxy had two satellite galaxies surrounding it.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/GalaxyMap_JediArchives.png/revision/latest?cb=20130726205128) [![The galaxy had two satellite galaxies surrounding it.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/GalaxyMap_JediArchives.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130726205128)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/GalaxyMap_JediArchives.png/revision/latest?cb=20130726205128) 

The galaxy had two satellite galaxies surrounding it.

 

The [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") had a diameter of 120,000 [light-years](/wiki/Light-year "Light-year"),[[4]](#cite_note-Altaya-4) over 400 billion [stars](/wiki/Star "Star"), more than 3.2 billion habitable [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system"),[[1]](#cite_note-VE-1) and at least two companion galaxies,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) the [Rishi Maze](/wiki/Rishi_Maze "Rishi Maze")[[16]](#cite_note-CL_2016-16) and the [far galaxy](/wiki/Far_galaxy "Far galaxy").[[17]](#cite_note-Filoni_Celebration-17) Outside its borders, the galaxy was surrounded by the [intergalactic void](/wiki/Intergalactic_void "Intergalactic void").[[18]](#cite_note-Part_4-18) Within its space, the galaxy was divided into several regions. The regions were subdivided into [sectors](/wiki/Sector "Sector") and then star systems which contained [planets](/wiki/Planet "Planet"). During the [reign](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), [oversectors](/wiki/Oversector "Oversector") were created and were composed of several sectors ruled by a [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff").[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8) Notable sectors/autonomous regions included the [Arkanis sector](/wiki/Arkanis_sector "Arkanis sector"), [Bothan Space](/wiki/Bothan_Space "Bothan Space"), [Centrality](/wiki/Centrality "Centrality"), [Corporate Sector](/wiki/Corporate_Sector "Corporate Sector"), [Gordian Reach](/wiki/Gordian_Reach "Gordian Reach"), [Greater Javin](/wiki/Greater_Javin "Greater Javin"), [Hapes Consortium](/wiki/Hapes_Consortium "Hapes Consortium"), [Hutt Space](/wiki/Hutt_Space "Hutt Space"), [Mandalorian Space](/wiki/Mandalore_sector "Mandalore sector"), [Moddell sector](/wiki/Moddell_sector "Moddell sector"), [Senex-Juvex](/wiki/Senex-Juvex "Senex-Juvex"), [Tion Cluster](/wiki/Tion_Cluster "Tion Cluster"),[[19]](#cite_note-TFABG-19) and [Western Reaches](/wiki/Western_Reaches "Western Reaches").[[11]](#cite_note-Star_Map-11)

The [Standard Galactic Grid](/wiki/Standard_Galactic_Grid "Standard Galactic Grid") was used to give the location of a galactic point in grid coordinates.[[20]](#cite_note-Rebel_Dossier-20) Areas of the galactic disk could be referred to as the galactic north, south, east and west.[[21]](#cite_note-Heir_to_the_Jedi-21) Notable points of interest were the fifty wonders of the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds"), thirty wonders of the [Mid Rim Territories](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") and the twenty-five wonders of the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories").[[6]](#cite_note-Catalyst-6) There were millions of [sentient](/wiki/Sentience "Sentience") [species](/wiki/Species "Species") in the galaxy.[[13]](#cite_note-TSWB-13) Millions of billions of individual beings called the galaxy home.[[22]](#cite_note-Through_the_Turbulence-22)

### Deep Core[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Deep Core](/wiki/Deep_Core "Deep Core")

:   "*It's crowded in there and things move fast.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[21]](#cite_note-Heir_to_the_Jedi-21)

The [Deep Core](/wiki/Deep_Core "Deep Core") served as the innermost and most brightly lit region of [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace"). It was densely-packed with stars, [nebulae](/wiki/Nebula "Nebula"), and other anomalies. As such, it was dangerous to navigate, leaving it relatively few explorers.[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23) It was from here that the ancient, super-massive [black hole](/wiki/Black_hole "Black hole")[[12]](#cite_note-Twilight_Company-12) known as the [Galactic Centre](/wiki/Galactic_Centre "Galactic Centre")[[24]](#cite_note-Falcon_36-24) bound the galaxy together.[[12]](#cite_note-Twilight_Company-12)

### Core Worlds[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds")

:   "*The Clone Wars did the unthinkable—it put the Core Worlds at risk. The insulated heart of the Republic had grown complacent in a sense of security and comfort. By war's end, the encroaching fear of Separatist attack reshaped the galaxy.*"
:   ―Janyor[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25)

 [![The Core World Coruscant was the historic center of galactic power.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Coruscant_system-TPM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200924030624) [![The Core World Coruscant was the historic center of galactic power.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Coruscant_system-TPM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200924030624)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Coruscant_system-TPM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200924030624) 

The Core World Coruscant was the historic center of galactic power.

 

The Core Worlds were home to the richest and most important worlds in the galaxy. Densely inhabited and located on the strategic ends of several major [trade lanes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"), its planets were hubs of fashion, education, finance, and technology. It is where the [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [species](/wiki/Species "Species") arguably[[1]](#cite_note-VE-1) began.[[26]](#cite_note-Uprising-26) It was from [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), [Corellia](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia"), [Kuat](/wiki/Kuat "Kuat"), [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime"), and other systems that the fate of the galaxy was often decided.[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23)

An attack on the Core Worlds was virtually inconceivable during the [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era"); according to the [Bith](/wiki/Bith "Bith") [artist](/wiki/Artist "Artist") [Janyor](/wiki/Janyor "Janyor"), the "sense of security and comfort" created an atmosphere of complacency within the heartland of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"). Toward the end of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars") though Core Worlders became increasingly fearful of a direct attack by the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems").[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25)

### Colonies[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Colonies](/wiki/Colonies "Colonies")

The [Colonies](/wiki/Colonies "Colonies") consisted of worlds colonized by the Core. Many of its planets sat along major trade routes, and were extremely wealthy. Notable planets included [Abednedo](/wiki/Abednedo_(planet) "Abednedo (planet)"),[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23) [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia "Cato Neimoidia"), and [Carida](/wiki/Carida "Carida").[[19]](#cite_note-TFABG-19)

### Inner Rim Territories[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Inner Rim Territories](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories")

When first settled, the [Inner Rim Territories](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories") served as the frontier of galactic civilization for [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century"), known simply as "the Rim." As colonization spread outwards, Inner Rim worlds prospered. Notable planets included [Bestine](/wiki/Bestine_IV "Bestine IV"), [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon"), [Thyferra](/wiki/Thyferra "Thyferra"), and [Taanab](/wiki/Taanab "Taanab").[[19]](#cite_note-TFABG-19)

### Expansion Region[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Expansion Region](/wiki/Expansion_Region "Expansion Region")

The [Expansion Region](/wiki/Expansion_Region "Expansion Region") contained many newer colonies sponsored by their coreward neighbors. Notable planets included [Umbara](/wiki/Umbara "Umbara"), [Mimban](/wiki/Mimban "Mimban"),[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23)[[19]](#cite_note-TFABG-19) and the [mining](/wiki/Mining "Mining") station known as the [Ring of Kafrene](/wiki/Ring_of_Kafrene "Ring of Kafrene").[[27]](#cite_note-RO_World_Locations-27)

### Mid Rim Territories[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Mid Rim Territories](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories")

 [![The planet Naboo was located in the Mid Rim Territories.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/TheedPalace_night.png/revision/latest?cb=20130121050719) [![The planet Naboo was located in the Mid Rim Territories.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/TheedPalace_night.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130121050719)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/TheedPalace_night.png/revision/latest?cb=20130121050719) 

The planet Naboo was located in the Mid Rim Territories.

 

The Mid Rim Territories were a tranquil region of space that brimmed with varied galactic worlds that boasted successful governments and thriving economies. Distance from the Core gave these worlds less fame or notoriety than planets closer to the galactic center.[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23) The Mid Rim was unofficially considered the lawful extent of the Galactic Republic and Galactic Empire.[[12]](#cite_note-Twilight_Company-12)[[1]](#cite_note-VE-1) Spillover [piracy](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") from the Outer Rim affected the region.[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23) Those headed towards the Outer Rim saw it as the last taste of civilization, while those heading corewards saw it as the last grasp of frontier living.[[28]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-28) Notable planets included [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"), [Malastare](/wiki/Malastare "Malastare"), [Bothawui](/wiki/Bothawui "Bothawui"), [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"), [Ruusan](/wiki/Ruusan "Ruusan"), [Ringo Vinda](/wiki/Ringo_Vinda "Ringo Vinda"), and [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell").[[19]](#cite_note-TFABG-19)

### Outer Rim Territories[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories")

:   "*The Outer Rim is a lawless place.*"
:   ―[Jennica Pierce](/wiki/Jennica_Pierce "Jennica Pierce")[[29]](#cite_note-Allies-29)

 [![The Outer Rim was home to worlds such as the desert planet of Tatooine.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/Mos_Eisley.png/revision/latest?cb=20121208215412) [![The Outer Rim was home to worlds such as the desert planet of Tatooine.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/Mos_Eisley.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121208215412)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/Mos_Eisley.png/revision/latest?cb=20121208215412) 

The Outer Rim was home to worlds such as the desert planet of Tatooine.

 

The largest[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23) region of the known galaxy, the Outer Rim Territories were considered to be lawless, strange, and savage. Criminal organizations, including the [Hutt Clan](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan") of [Hutt Space](/wiki/Hutt_Space "Hutt Space"), the [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun "Black Sun"), [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate"), and [Zygerrian](/wiki/Zygerrian "Zygerrian") [enslavers](/wiki/Enslaver "Enslaver") operated in abundance within the region.[[1]](#cite_note-VE-1) Notable worlds included [Arkanis](/wiki/Arkanis "Arkanis"), [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala"), [Kessel](/wiki/Kessel "Kessel"), [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth"), [Eriadu](/wiki/Eriadu "Eriadu"), [Sullust](/wiki/Sullust "Sullust"), [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis"), [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"), [Crait](/wiki/Crait "Crait"), [Nal Hutta](/wiki/Nal_Hutta "Nal Hutta"), [Cantonica](/wiki/Cantonica "Cantonica"), [Hoth](/wiki/Hoth "Hoth"), [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal"), [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah"), [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor"), [Nar Shaddaa](/wiki/Nar_Shaddaa "Nar Shaddaa"), [Florrum](/wiki/Florrum "Florrum"), [Yavin 4](/wiki/Yavin_4 "Yavin 4"), [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami"), [Scarif](/wiki/Scarif "Scarif"), [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia"), [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir"), and [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine").[[19]](#cite_note-TFABG-19)

### Unknown Regions[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions")

:   "*The Unknown Regions are vast.*"
:   ―[Caluan Ematt](/wiki/Caluan_Ematt "Caluan Ematt")[[30]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-30)

 [![Mysterious and largely unexplored, the Unknown Regions was located beyond the known galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Unknown_Regions_TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210528200552) [![Mysterious and largely unexplored, the Unknown Regions was located beyond the known galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Unknown_Regions_TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210528200552)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Unknown_Regions_TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210528200552) 

Mysterious and largely unexplored, the Unknown Regions was located beyond the known galaxy.

 

The [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions") was composed of the westward arm of the galaxy that was mapped, but largely unexplored.[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23) Solar storms, rogue magnetospheres, black holes, [gravity wells](/wiki/Gravity_well "Gravity well"), and other handicaps to [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") travel left it largely unexplored throughout galactic history.[[31]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-31) Mysterious species shrouded in myth, such the [Chiss](/wiki/Chiss "Chiss")[[32]](#cite_note-Thrawn-32) and [Grysk](/wiki/Grysk "Grysk"),[[33]](#cite_note-Thrawn:_Alliances-33) as well as the deeply-religious [Kilji](/wiki/Kilji "Kilji") species originated from the Unknown Regions. Notable planets included [Csilla](/wiki/Csilla "Csilla"),[[19]](#cite_note-TFABG-19) [Ilum](/wiki/Ilum "Ilum"),[[34]](#cite_note-Ultimate-34) [Rakata Prime](/wiki/Rakata_Prime "Rakata Prime"),[[28]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-28) [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol"),[[35]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-35) and [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To").[[36]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-36)

### Wild Space[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Wild Space](/wiki/Wild_Space "Wild Space")

:   "*Those systems are beyond the Outer Rim, in Wild Space. Not on any map.*"
:   ―Kanan Jarrus[[37]](#cite_note-Lasat-37)

Unlike other regions of the galaxy, [Wild Space](/wiki/Wild_Space "Wild Space") existed along the entire circumference of the galactic disk and on the borderlands of the Unknown Regions.[[19]](#cite_note-TFABG-19) It was inhabited by [sentient](/wiki/Sentience "Sentience") species but not fully charted, explored, and civilized.[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8)[[11]](#cite_note-Star_Map-11) Explorers and [cartographers](/wiki/Cartographer "Cartographer") sought their fortune here at their peril.[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23)

## History[]

### Early galactic civilization[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Timeline of galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history")

:   "*Societal memories and official calendars started fresh, and the time before this rebirth was forgotten as a dark age, lumped into a collective whole known as the 'Old Republic.'*"
:   ―Janyor[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25)

 [![The Old Republic was an early incarnation of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/OldRepublicEmblem.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250720043825) [![The Old Republic was an early incarnation of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/OldRepublicEmblem.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20250720043825)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/OldRepublicEmblem.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250720043825) 

The Old Republic was an early incarnation of the Galactic Republic.

 

The [history of the galaxy](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history") spans many [millennia](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium"). Approximately twenty-five millennia before the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"), one or more ancestor species discovered hyperspace travel. This invention opened the galaxy up for exploration and travel.[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8)

To navigate the unimaginably large distances between star systems, spacecraft utilized a [hyperdrive](/wiki/Hyperdrive "Hyperdrive"). This [propulsion system](/wiki/Engine "Engine") allowed travel through hyperspace, an alternate dimension where a [starship](/wiki/Starship "Starship") could take advantage of the wrinkles in the fabric of [spacetime](/wiki/Space-time_continuum "Space-time continuum") to reduce journey [time](/wiki/Time "Time") and distance significantly, effectively "jumping" from point to point without having to travel directly between them.[[38]](#cite_note-LOTJ-38) Galactic travelers used [hyperspace sextants](/wiki/Hyperspace_sextant "Hyperspace sextant") for navigating hyperspace roughly four thousand years before the [Cold War](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War").[[28]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-28)

In ancient times, beings from a [far galaxy](/wiki/Far_galaxy "Far galaxy") built a [reflex point](/wiki/Seatos_reflex_point "Seatos reflex point") on the planet [Seatos](/wiki/Seatos "Seatos") which [pointed the way](/wiki/Pathway_to_Peridea "Pathway to Peridea") to an extragalactic location known to [Peridea](/wiki/Peridea "Peridea"). While some such as former [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Baylan Skoll](/wiki/Baylan_Skoll "Baylan Skoll") regarded Peridea as a fairytale, [Nightsister](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") survivor Lady [Morgan Elsbeth](/wiki/Morgan_Elsbeth "Morgan Elsbeth") regarded Peridea as a real place that was the ancient homeworld of her ancestors.[[39]](#cite_note-Ahsoka_2-39) A [star map](/wiki/Arcana_Star_Map "Arcana Star Map") pointing the way to the far galaxy was also stored inside a [Nightsister stronghold](/wiki/Nightsisters%27_Temple "Nightsisters' Temple") on [Arcana](/wiki/Arcana "Arcana").[[40]](#cite_note-Ahsoka_1-40)

The [Old Republic-era](/wiki/Old_Republic-era "Old Republic-era")[[41]](#cite_note-Official_Guide-41) began with the formation of the early Republic[[13]](#cite_note-TSWB-13)[[42]](#cite_note-Old_Galactic_Republic-42) around [25,000 BBY](/wiki/25,000_BBY "25,000 BBY").[[43]](#cite_note-25,000_BBY_Date_Note-43) The Republic was founded by the [Core Founders](/wiki/Core_Founder "Core Founder"), a group of twenty-two Core Worlds which included the planet [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan").[[44]](#cite_note-Rising_Storm-44)

 [![The Jedi Order was founded by the Prime Jedi thousands of years before the Battle of Yavin.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Prime_Jedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220413031517) [![The Jedi Order was founded by the Prime Jedi thousands of years before the Battle of Yavin.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Prime_Jedi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220413031517)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Prime_Jedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220413031517) 

The Jedi Order was founded by the Prime Jedi thousands of years before the Battle of Yavin.

 

The [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") was also formed around 25,000 BBY.[[43]](#cite_note-25,000_BBY_Date_Note-43) A noble group of [Force-sensitives](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") capable of harnessing the [powers](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"),[[45]](#cite_note-Jedi_Order_DB-45) the Order originated with the [Prime Jedi](/wiki/Prime_Jedi "Prime Jedi") on the planet Ahch-To, where the [first Jedi Temple](/wiki/First_Jedi_Temple "First Jedi Temple") was built.[[36]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-36) As told by [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), "the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") served as the guardians of peace and justice for over a thousand generations in the Old Republic."[[46]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-46) Later, a sect of Force-sensitives who followed the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") split from the Jedi[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8) to form the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") during the [Hundred-Year Darkness](/wiki/Hundred-Year_Darkness "Hundred-Year Darkness").[[47]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_9-47) In one of their wars, the world [Malachor](/wiki/Malachor "Malachor") was devastated during the [Great Scourge of Malachor](/wiki/Great_Scourge_of_Malachor "Great Scourge of Malachor"), which left the battlefield littered with the petrified corpses of the Sith and Jedi combatants.[[48]](#cite_note-Twilight_of_the_Apprentice-48)

The Sith built an [Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire") through the use of [slave labor](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery").[[49]](#cite_note-EfK-49)[[31]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-31) During their period of galactic dominance, the Sith built a [shrine](/wiki/Shrine_in_the_Depths "Shrine in the Depths") on Coruscant. The [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") was constructed over the foundations of the shrine subsequent to the [Jedi victory](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant_(Sith_war) "Battle of Coruscant (Sith war)") that drove the Sith from Coruscant.[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8)

 [![The Sith Order survived for generations under Darth Bane's Rule of Two.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/BaneSidiousVader.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211127170520) [![The Sith Order survived for generations under Darth Bane's Rule of Two.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/BaneSidiousVader.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20211127170520)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/BaneSidiousVader.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211127170520) 

The Sith Order survived for generations under Darth Bane's Rule of Two.

 

The [last conflict](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") between the Jedi Knights[[50]](#cite_note-Bane_Galactic_Files-50) and the Sith ended with the [defeat of the Sith](/wiki/Defeat_of_the_Sith "Defeat of the Sith")[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8) on the Mid Rim planet[[51]](#cite_note-Visual_Encyclopedia-51) [Ruusan](/wiki/Ruusan "Ruusan")[[52]](#cite_note-HC_29-52) in [1032 BBY](/wiki/1032_BBY "1032 BBY").[[53]](#cite_note-Timelines-53) The victory of the Republic was so complete[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25) that the Jedi believed the Sith to be extinct. However, the Sith lineage continued through a sole survivor, Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane") whose [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two") ensured the continuation of the Sith[[54]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-54) for a millennium in [secret](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan").[[55]](#cite_note-Episode_I-55) Bane's [death](/wiki/Death "Death") by the hand of his [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice")[[56]](#cite_note-SOTS-56) [Darth Zannah](/wiki/Darth_Zannah "Darth Zannah")[[57]](#cite_note-HC_2-57) began a tradition in which the apprentice finished their training by killing their [Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master").[[56]](#cite_note-SOTS-56)

In addition to the Sith,[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25) the [Zygerrian Slave Empire](/wiki/Zygerrian_Slave_Empire "Zygerrian Slave Empire")[[58]](#cite_note-DBZygerrian-58) and the [Mandalorians](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") were adversaries of the Jedi Order.[[59]](#cite_note-Mandalore_Plot-59) The Jedi [defeated](/wiki/Jedi%E2%80%93Zygerrian_conflict "Jedi–Zygerrian conflict") the [Zygerrians](/wiki/Zygerrian "Zygerrian"),[[58]](#cite_note-DBZygerrian-58) but lost to the Mandalorians with the [sacking of the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Sacking_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Sacking of the Jedi Temple").[[59]](#cite_note-Mandalore_Plot-59) In the sack, the Jedi Order lost one of their [artifacts](/wiki/Jedi_artifact "Jedi artifact"), the [Darksaber](/wiki/Darksaber "Darksaber"). Forged by [Tarre Vizsla](/wiki/Tarre_Vizsla "Tarre Vizsla"), the first Mandalorian ever inducted into the Jedi Order,[[60]](#cite_note-Trials_of_the_Darksaber-60) the Darksaber was taken from the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") on Coruscant by members of [House Vizsla](/wiki/House_Vizsla "House Vizsla").[[59]](#cite_note-Mandalore_Plot-59) The Jedi eventually won the [Mandalorian-Jedi War](/wiki/Mandalorian-Jedi_War "Mandalorian-Jedi War"),[[60]](#cite_note-Trials_of_the_Darksaber-60) a conflict that left the planet [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore") [devastated](/wiki/Annihilation "Annihilation") and transformed into a largely uninhabitable wasteland.[[61]](#cite_note-Mandalorian_super_commando-61)

### The Galactic Republic[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era")

#### Forming a new era[]

:   "*The Republic victory was so definitive that it reinvented itself, resettling its capital on Coruscant after a devastating ouster. History reset its chrono on this date, and from that moment, the modern Galactic Republic was born.*"
:   ―Janyor[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25)

 [![Under the protection of the Jedi Order, the modern Galactic Republic presided over a millennium of peace.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/CoruscantBG-SWcom.png/revision/latest?cb=20200416222516) [![Under the protection of the Jedi Order, the modern Galactic Republic presided over a millennium of peace.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/CoruscantBG-SWcom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200416222516)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/CoruscantBG-SWcom.png/revision/latest?cb=20200416222516) 

Under the protection of the Jedi Order, the modern Galactic Republic presided over a millennium of peace.

 

The defeat of the Sith brought about the formation of the modern Republic[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25) in 1032 BBY.[[62]](#cite_note-Galactic_Republic_Date_Note-62) This version of the Republic, while viewed as the "latest evolution" of a millennia-old [democratic](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") [polity](/wiki/Politics "Politics"), was nevertheless a new beginning for galactic society. Its establishment therefore served as the epoch of the new era, while the history prior to the reinvention of the Republic was ultimately lost and referred to as the "Old Republic."[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25)

As the home of the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), Coruscant served as the political [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of the galaxy.[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25) The Republic was the dominant galactic government for a thousand years until the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") and the [Clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") Wars.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) During the Republic's reign, the Core Worlds underwent a wave of expansion by settling new worlds and establishing trading colonies. In the process, they also cut deals with native populations or simply overran them.[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8) A millennium before [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"),[[63]](#cite_note-Yavin_Code_Date_Note-63) the [Yavin Code](/wiki/Yavin_Code "Yavin Code") was established during the [Yavin Convention](/wiki/Yavin_Convention "Yavin Convention") to govern the treatment of [prisoners](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner").[[64]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-64)

#### High Republic Era[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era")

When the [Evereni](/wiki/Evereni "Evereni") left their [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of [Everon](/wiki/Everon "Everon"), they were surprised to find other life-forms and, due to their natural inclination to distrust others, began to wipe out the beings they encountered, turning themselves into outlaws and forcing them to act through more covert means.[[65]](#cite_note-EotS1-65) During the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"), the galaxy was believed to be at peace, resulting in less of a need for military forces. Protected by the Jedi and the [Republic Defense Coalition](/wiki/Republic_Defense_Coalition "Republic Defense Coalition"), the Republic expanded into the Outer Rim to spread its era of ambition and [Great Works](/wiki/Great_Works "Great Works"), yet it would instead find itself in [conflict](/wiki/Nihil_conflict "Nihil conflict") with the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil") after the [Great Hyperspace Disaster](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_Disaster "Great Hyperspace Disaster")[[66]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-66) in [232 BBY](/wiki/232_BBY "232 BBY").[[53]](#cite_note-Timelines-53) In truth, the Nihil were pawns of a [family of Evereni](/wiki/Ro_family "Ro family") who wanted revenge on the Jedi and Republic for past events[[65]](#cite_note-EotS1-65) that stretched back to the days of the [Path of the Open Hand](/wiki/Path_of_the_Open_Hand "Path of the Open Hand") cult:[[67]](#cite_note-Path_Ven-67) over a century prior,[[53]](#cite_note-Timelines-53) the Path had entered into conflict with the Jedi due to their opposing views on the Force, which the Path believed no living being was allowed to manipulate. To secure an advantage over the Jedi, [Mother](/wiki/Mother_(title) "Mother (title)") [Elecia Zeveron](/wiki/Elecia_Zeveron "Elecia Zeveron") unleashed beings known as the Nameless, which hunted Force-sensitives and were controlled by a [set of rods](/wiki/Nameless_control_rods "Nameless control rods").[[67]](#cite_note-Path_Ven-67)

First unleashing a [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai")[[67]](#cite_note-Path_Ven-67) known later as the [Great Leveler](/wiki/Great_Leveler "Great Leveler"),[[44]](#cite_note-Rising_Storm-44) the Path journeyed to the [Nameless homeworld](/wiki/Sophros "Sophros") after stirring the [Battle of Jedha](/wiki/Battle_of_Jedha "Battle of Jedha") into being. On the world, informally known as Planet X, the Path discovered more Nameless eggs, but one team member, [Bokana Koss](/wiki/Bokana_Koss "Bokana Koss"), experienced a Force vision that warned him beings known as the [Under-Dwellers](/wiki/Under-Dweller "Under-Dweller") would take advantage of their mission to spread across the galaxy as a [blight](/wiki/Blight "Blight"), with that blight "chaining" and trying to destroy the Force itself if unleashed. Ignoring his warning, the Path made it off Planet X despite the efforts of a being known as the [protector](/wiki/Protector_(Planet_X) "Protector (Planet X)") and [the Veil](/wiki/The_Veil_(Planet_X) "The Veil (Planet X)"). In the ensuing [Night of Sorrow](/wiki/Night_of_Sorrow "Night of Sorrow"), the Path, reformed into the [Path of the Closed Fist](/wiki/Path_of_the_Closed_Fist "Path of the Closed Fist"), warred with the Jedi and their allies until [Path Guide](/wiki/Guide_of_the_Closed_Fist "Guide of the Closed Fist") [Marda Ro](/wiki/Marda_Ro "Marda Ro")—who was horrified at the way the Nameless feasted upon people, witnessed that the Nameless targeted members of her own order without regard if they happened to be Force-sensitive, and realized the Mother had lied to her—wiped out the Nameless with the exception of the Leveler. After killing Zeveron with the Leveler and escaping with the beast,[[67]](#cite_note-Path_Ven-67) Ro forged the original incarnation of the Nihil[[68]](#cite_note-Temptation-68) and passed her revenge down over the generations[[65]](#cite_note-EotS1-65) with the hope they would at last "free" the Force."[[67]](#cite_note-Path_Ven-67)

Those efforts culminated in the finalized Nihil and[[65]](#cite_note-EotS1-65) Marda's descendant[[68]](#cite_note-Temptation-68) [Marchion Ro](/wiki/Marchion_Ro "Marchion Ro"),[[65]](#cite_note-EotS1-65) who claimed to still practice the family rituals[[44]](#cite_note-Rising_Storm-44) and was dedicated to their revenge,[[66]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-66) but, perhaps without realizing it, was most interesting in securing his own freedom from anyone who would chain him down.[[69]](#cite_note-EotS2-69) Marchion led the Nihil through war with the Republic and Jedi and rediscovered the Great Leveler,[[44]](#cite_note-Rising_Storm-44) in time [venturing to Planet X](/wiki/Mission_to_Planet_X "Mission to Planet X") himself with the Nihil to claim even more Nameless. Thanks to Ro, the Nihil [brought down](/wiki/Destruction_of_Starlight_Beacon "Destruction of Starlight Beacon") Supreme Chancellor [Lina Soh](/wiki/Lina_Soh "Lina Soh")'s great [Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Starlight_Beacon "Starlight Beacon") project and [claimed](/wiki/Deployment_of_the_stormseeds "Deployment of the stormseeds") an entire segment of the galaxy as [Nihil-controlled space](/wiki/Occlusion_Zone "Occlusion Zone").[[69]](#cite_note-EotS2-69) As the Jedi and Republic continued their conflict against the Nihil and worked to free the sectors the pirates had claimed,[[68]](#cite_note-Temptation-68) however, the blight foretold by Koss[[67]](#cite_note-Path_Ven-67) was discovered by both the Jedi and Nihil.[[68]](#cite_note-Temptation-68)

#### Late Republic Era[]

As the Republic continued along, corruption began to take greater power in the Galactic Senate, while [megacorporations](/wiki/Megacorporation "Megacorporation") like the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") were granted representation within the government body.[[55]](#cite_note-Episode_I-55) The Jedi Order grew to be unwilling to challenge the corruption of the Senate at large[[70]](#cite_note-TOTJ_Choices-70) and increasingly isolated from the greater galaxy[[71]](#cite_note-The_Living_Force-71) even though discontent with the Republic and its corruption emerged.[[70]](#cite_note-TOTJ_Choices-70)[[72]](#cite_note-Justice-72)

 [![The Sith Lord Darth Sidious masterminded his own rise to power as Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/Sidious_hologram.png/revision/latest?cb=20200921210616) [![The Sith Lord Darth Sidious masterminded his own rise to power as Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/Sidious_hologram.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200921210616)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/Sidious_hologram.png/revision/latest?cb=20200921210616) 

The Sith Lord Darth Sidious masterminded his own rise to power as Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine.

 

In the years leading up to the Clone Wars, [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") foresaw an upcoming conflict and, against the wishes of the Jedi Order, commissioned the [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") to create an [army](/wiki/Army "Army") of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") on [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino").[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7) In [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"),[[53]](#cite_note-Timelines-53) a dispute between the Republic and the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") over the [taxation](/wiki/Prop_31-814D "Prop 31-814D") of [trade routes](/wiki/Free_Trade_Zone "Free Trade Zone") to outlying systems led the Federation to impose a [blockade](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") on the Mid Rim world of Naboo. The Federation was eventually expelled by a coalition of [Naboo humans](/wiki/Naboo_(people) "Naboo (people)"), [Gungans](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan"), and Jedi. [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") of Naboo took advantage of the occupation of his [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") in order to succeed [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum") as [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor").[[55]](#cite_note-Episode_I-55) In secret, Palpatine was [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, who was dedicated to reestablishing the Sith’s rule of the galaxy.[[73]](#cite_note-Episode_III-73)

### The Clone Wars[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars")

:   "*For years, the Clone Wars raged across hundreds of worlds. The Jedi led their seemingly faithful clone troops in an onslaught of harrowing battles, their Order growing ever weaker.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[56]](#cite_note-SOTS-56)

 [![The Separatist Crisis led to open war between the Galactic Republic and the Confederacy of Independent Systems.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20170325151752) [![The Separatist Crisis led to open war between the Galactic Republic and the Confederacy of Independent Systems.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170325151752)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20170325151752) 

The Separatist Crisis led to open war between the Galactic Republic and the Confederacy of Independent Systems.

 

The [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") was formed between [24 BBY](/wiki/24_BBY "24 BBY") and [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY")[[74]](#cite_note-CIS_Formation_Date_Note-74) as a result of widespread dissatisfaction with the Republic. The Separatist movement was led by [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), a former Jedi Master who became Darth Sidious' second Sith apprentice as Darth Tyranus. During the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"), several thousand star systems and corporations declared their intention to leave the Republic. The discovery of a clone army on Kamino and the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") on Geonosis set the stage for the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"), which became the catalyst of the Clone Wars. At the urging of [Junior Representative](/wiki/Junior_Representative "Junior Representative") [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks"), the Senate transferred [emergency powers](/wiki/Emergency_Powers_Act "Emergency Powers Act") to Chancellor Palpatine, who used his new-found powers to formally create the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic").[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_II-7)

 [![During the Clone Wars, Republic and Separatist armies fought numerous battles across the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5c/Battle_of_Christophsis.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013044237) [![During the Clone Wars, Republic and Separatist armies fought numerous battles across the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5c/Battle_of_Christophsis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121013044237)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5c/Battle_of_Christophsis.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013044237) 

During the Clone Wars, Republic and Separatist armies fought numerous battles across the galaxy.

 

The Clone Wars engulfed much of the galaxy for the next three years.[[23]](#cite_note-SWGA-23) The Jedi-led [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") and [Separatist forces](/wiki/Confederacy_military "Confederacy military") fought on multiple worlds and fronts including [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis"),[[75]](#cite_note-TCW_film-75) Ryloth,[[76]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-76) Umbara,[[77]](#cite_note-Darkness_on_Umbara-77) Onderon,[[78]](#cite_note-A_War_on_Two_Fronts-78) Coruscant, [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"), and Kashyyyk. The Confederacy of Independent Systems collapsed with the [deaths](/wiki/Death "Death") of Dooku, [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"), and the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") [on Mustafar](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar"). Chancellor Palpatine, having accused the Jedi Order of [treason](/wiki/Treason "Treason"), commanded the Grand Army of the Republic to execute [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), resulting in many Jedi being gunned down by their clone troopers. With the Jedi Order effectively destroyed, Palpatine was [proclaimed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") as [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") and the Republic was reorganized into the first [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire").[[73]](#cite_note-Episode_III-73)

 [![With the Jedi all but destroyed, the Republic was supplanted by the first Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/AmeddaJediEradicationCeremony-2017DarthVader1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170622194336) [![With the Jedi all but destroyed, the Republic was supplanted by the first Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/AmeddaJediEradicationCeremony-2017DarthVader1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170622194336)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/AmeddaJediEradicationCeremony-2017DarthVader1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170622194336) 

With the Jedi all but destroyed, the Republic was supplanted by the first Galactic Empire.

 

Most of the Jedi were killed in the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge").[[46]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-46) Whereas the Order comprised ten thousand Jedi Knights at the time of the Clone Wars, only a few survivors remained during the height of Imperial rule.[[79]](#cite_note-The_Siege_of_Lothal-79) The Jedi were vilified by Imperial [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda"), with [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda") publicly denouncing them while hosting a [celebration](/wiki/Celebration_marking_the_eradication_of_the_Jedi_Order "Celebration marking the eradication of the Jedi Order") of their eradication at the Jedi Temple on Coruscant.[[80]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-80) The Jedi who survived the initial purge were scattered across the galaxy. Master Kenobi fled to Tatooine,[[46]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-46) Grand Master [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") retreated to Dagobah, a wild and swampy world;[[81]](#cite_note-Episode_V-81) and Padawan [Cal Kestis](/wiki/Cal_Kestis "Cal Kestis") joined the [Scrapper Guild](/wiki/Scrapper_Guild "Scrapper Guild") on [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca").[[82]](#cite_note-JFO-82)

A number of Jedi even joined the Empire. The [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius"), a group of [Jedi hunters](/wiki/Jedi_hunter "Jedi hunter") who served the Empire, was composed of fallen Jedi such as the [Second Sister](/wiki/Second_Sister "Second Sister"), who was once Trilla Suduri of the Jedi Order.[[82]](#cite_note-JFO-82) Kenobi’s former apprentice Jedi Knight [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") became Sidious' final apprentice;[[73]](#cite_note-Episode_III-73) as Darth Vader and was instrumental in the Great Jedi Purge.[[46]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-46)

### The Galactic Empire[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era")

:   "*Under the Sith… [the galaxy] is a* pyramid*. Everyone climbing to the same place, pushing others down so they can ascend. And at its peak, someone waits ready to* destroy *anyone who would dare approach. The only* truly free *person in the entire galaxy.* Emperor Palpatine*. His name, his* Sith *name, is* Darth Sidious*. The name of his apprentice is* Darth Vader*. They are the two* most powerful *people in the galaxy.*"
:   ―[Qi'ra](/wiki/Qi%27ra "Qi'ra")[[83]](#cite_note-Crimson_1-83)

 [![As Emperor Palpatine, Darth Sidious ruled the galaxy with Darth Vader as his apprentice and enforcer.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Moff_Tarkin.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208042141) [![As Emperor Palpatine, Darth Sidious ruled the galaxy with Darth Vader as his apprentice and enforcer.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Moff_Tarkin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130208042141)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/Moff_Tarkin.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208042141) 

As Emperor Palpatine, Darth Sidious ruled the galaxy with Darth Vader as his apprentice and enforcer.

 

The [fascist](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism") Galactic Empire became the dominant government of the galaxy for the next two and a half [decades](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade"). The Empire assumed control over galactic society, interplanetary economies, the [HoloNet](/wiki/HoloNet "HoloNet"), and a sprawling [Imperial Military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military").[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25) As Galactic Emperor, Palpatine wielded considerable power over the Empire's military, resources, and inhabitants. The revamped [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate") saw more of its powers being transferred to planetary and regional [governors](/wiki/Governor "Governor") who had been appointed by the Empire.[[84]](#cite_note-Rebels_Visual_Guide-84)

The [Imperial Survey Corps](/wiki/Imperial_Survey_Corps "Imperial Survey Corps") took an interest in exploring the uncharted reaches of space, including the Unknown Regions[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8) and Wild Space. As a result, the demand for maps and cartographers exponentially increased. This allowed explorers such as [Auric](/wiki/Auric_Graf "Auric Graf") and [Rhyssa Graf](/wiki/Rhyssa_Graf "Rhyssa Graf") to make a decent living from selling maps until they were kidnapped by the Imperial [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Visler Korda](/wiki/Visler_Korda "Visler Korda").[[85]](#cite_note-Escape-85) In addition, the Empire created a galactic-wide network of [Imperial Academies](/wiki/Imperial_Academy "Imperial Academy") to indoctrinate and train youths to serve in the Imperial Military.[[86]](#cite_note-Edge_of_the_Galaxy-86) In secret, the Empire embarked on an ambitious [program](/wiki/Project_Stardust "Project Stardust") to create a planet-destroying [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon") called the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station").[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8)

 [![The New Order was maintained through Imperial propaganda and military might.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/StrengthAndObedience-SWPropaganda.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161214212040) [![The New Order was maintained through Imperial propaganda and military might.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/StrengthAndObedience-SWPropaganda.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161214212040)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/StrengthAndObedience-SWPropaganda.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161214212040) 

The New Order was maintained through Imperial propaganda and military might.

 

The Empire also expropriated land and resources and ruthlessly stamped out dissent. HoloNet and other media became a [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda") medium for the Empire.[[86]](#cite_note-Edge_of_the_Galaxy-86) In addition, the Empire was [xenophobic](/wiki/Xenophobia "Xenophobia") and favored humans at the expense of [alien](/wiki/Alien "Alien") species. In the Imperial order, aliens were regarded as serfs, slaves, and obstacles needing to be tamed, removed, or ignored. Humans came to dominate the Imperial government and military while alien species, such as the [Wookiees](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") and the [Talz](/wiki/Talz "Talz") were enslaved.[[87]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-87) Other alien species such as the [Lasat](/wiki/Lasat "Lasat")[[88]](#cite_note-Droids_in_Distress-88) to make an example and the [Geonosians](/wiki/Geonosian "Geonosian") also [experienced](/wiki/Siege_of_Lasan "Siege of Lasan") [genocide](/wiki/Sterilization_of_Geonosis "Sterilization of Geonosis") to keep the Death Star secret.[[89]](#cite_note-Ghosts_of_Genosis-89) Despite this entrenched xenophobia, some aliens rose to positions of prominence in the Empire such as the [Chagrian](/wiki/Chagrian "Chagrian") [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda"),[[8]](#cite_note-Tarkin-8) the [Pau'an](/wiki/Pau%27an "Pau'an") [Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"),[[90]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Old_Masters-90) and the Chiss [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo").[[91]](#cite_note-Steps_Into_Shadow-91)

In [10 BBY](/wiki/10_BBY "10 BBY"),[[53]](#cite_note-Timelines-53) [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") set a new galactic record by making the [Kessel Run](/wiki/Kessel_Run "Kessel Run") in less than twelve parsecs aboard the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")*, which he later acquired from [Lando Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian"). Solo and his companions his partner [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca"), his lover [Lady](/wiki/Lady "Lady") [Qi'ra](/wiki/Qi%27ra "Qi'ra"), his mentor [Tobias Beckett](/wiki/Tobias_Beckett "Tobias Beckett"), Calrissian, and [L3-37](/wiki/L3-37 "L3-37") had earlier [stolen](/wiki/Raid_on_Kessel "Raid on Kessel") [coaxium](/wiki/Coaxium "Coaxium") from the spice mining world of [Kessel](/wiki/Kessel "Kessel") in order to settle Beckett's debts to the [Crimson Dawn](/wiki/Crimson_Dawn "Crimson Dawn") syndicate. Solo and his companions were later [involved](/wiki/Showdown_on_Savareen "Showdown on Savareen") in the death of Crimson Dawn public leader [Dryden Vos](/wiki/Dryden_Vos "Dryden Vos").[[92]](#cite_note-Solo-92)

### The Galactic Civil War[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War")

:   "*The Galactic Civil War was not a battle for territory. It was a struggle for the hearts and minds of the galaxy.*"
:   ―Janyor[[25]](#cite_note-Propaganda-25)

 [![The Galactic Civil War was a conflict between the Galactic Empire and the Alliance to Restore the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Scarif_Battle_GaG_cover_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20190621035447) [![The Galactic Civil War was a conflict between the Galactic Empire and the Alliance to Restore the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Scarif_Battle_GaG_cover_art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190621035447)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Scarif_Battle_GaG_cover_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20190621035447) 

The Galactic Civil War was a conflict between the Galactic Empire and the Alliance to Restore the Republic.

 

As the Empire tightened its grip on the galaxy, [resistance movements](/wiki/Early_rebellion_against_the_Galactic_Empire "Early rebellion against the Galactic Empire") sprang up on a number of worlds. Most of these movements were strictly local, determined to free an individual planet or star system from Imperial rule.[[93]](#cite_note-Rebel_DB-93) Eventually, however, dissatisfaction and opposition to the Empire culminated in a scattered network of [rebel cells](/wiki/Rebel_cell_(disambiguation) "Rebel cell (disambiguation)"). In [4 BBY](/wiki/4_BBY "4 BBY"),[[94]](#cite_note-FAtG_Date-94) rebel cells [began](/wiki/Action_at_Mustafar "Action at Mustafar") to coalesce into larger groups such as the [Phoenix Cell](/wiki/Phoenix_Cell "Phoenix Cell"), ending a previous policy of maintaining secrecy[[95]](#cite_note-Fire_Across_the_Galaxy-95) and beginning the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War").[[96]](#cite_note-GCW_Date-96) As the Rebellion grew in power, some Imperial tacticians such as Thrawn[[91]](#cite_note-Steps_Into_Shadow-91) and [ISB Supervisor](/wiki/ISB_Supervisor "ISB Supervisor") Commander [Dedra Meero](/wiki/Dedra_Meero "Dedra Meero")[[97]](#cite_note-Announcement-97) realized the Empire was facing a galaxy-wide insurgency.[[91]](#cite_note-Steps_Into_Shadow-91)

In [2 BBY](/wiki/2_BBY "2 BBY"),[[53]](#cite_note-Timelines-53) the rebel cells [officially](/wiki/Declaration_of_the_Rebel_Alliance "Declaration of the Rebel Alliance") formed the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") under [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(Rebel_Alliance) "Chancellor (Rebel Alliance)") [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma")[[98]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-98) and [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy "Viceroy") [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa").[[93]](#cite_note-Rebel_DB-93) In [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"),[[53]](#cite_note-Timelines-53) in an attempt to obtain the [Death Star plans](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans"), the Rebel Alliance launched an [attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Scarif "Battle of Scarif") on Scarif,[[99]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-99) which marked the first victory for the Rebellion in the Galactic Civil War. Shortly later,[[46]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-46) in 1 BBY,[[100]](#cite_note-Atlas_Updated-100) the Empire [destroyed](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan") the planet Alderaan under Emperor Palpatine’s protege Governor [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") to showcase the power of the Death Star. In response, the Rebel Alliance used the stolen Death Star plans to destroy the Death Star during the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin").[[46]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-46)

 [![With the Emperor slain and the second Death Star destroyed, the Battle of Endor marked a turning point in the Galactic Civil War.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/X-wings-and-DS2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230815200035) [![With the Emperor slain and the second Death Star destroyed, the Battle of Endor marked a turning point in the Galactic Civil War.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/X-wings-and-DS2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230815200035)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/X-wings-and-DS2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230815200035) 

With the Emperor slain and the second Death Star destroyed, the Battle of Endor marked a turning point in the Galactic Civil War.

 

For the next four years, the galaxy was locked in a civil war between the Empire and the Rebel Alliance. Fighting took place at locations like the Mid Rim, Sullust,[[12]](#cite_note-Twilight_Company-12) [Hoth](/wiki/Hoth "Hoth"), and [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City").[[81]](#cite_note-Episode_V-81) Crimson Dawn would also re-emerge and launch a [war against the Sith](/wiki/War_against_the_Sith "War against the Sith"), which would end in its defeat at the hands of Sidious and Vader.[[101]](#cite_note-Hidden_Empire_5-101) In the wake of Crimson Dawn's defeat, a rogue droid known as the [Scourge](/wiki/Scourge "Scourge") emerged and spread an [infection of droids and cyborgs](/wiki/Scourge_crisis "Scourge crisis")[[102]](#cite_note-Dark_Droids_1-102) with the ultimate goal of taking over the Force, only to be opposed by the [warrior-priest droid](/wiki/Warrior-priest_droid "Warrior-priest droid") [Ajax Sigma](/wiki/Ajax_Sigma "Ajax Sigma").[[103]](#cite_note-Dark_Droids_Target_Vader-103) In secret, the Emperor commissioned the construction of a [second Death Star](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station") above Endor and [laid a trap](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") for the Rebel Alliance in a calculated gamble. However, Vader’s son Jedi Knight [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") managed to redeem him before he saved his son by fulfilling his destiny of killing Emperor Palpatine, destroying the Sith again,[[104]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-104) and bringing balance back to the Force.[[105]](#cite_note-Luke_Bio_Gallery-105) The death of Emperor Palpatine and the destruction of the Death Star II had a cataclysmic effect on the galaxy.[[106]](#cite_note-Aftermath-106)

### The New Republic[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era")

:   "*Join us in the foundation of a new Republic to be shaped by the will of the governed. Claim your freedom and your future. Help is on the way.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[26]](#cite_note-Uprising-26)

 [![The founding of the New Republic marked the dawn of a new era in galactic history.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/A_New_Dawn-SWP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170110083833) [![The founding of the New Republic marked the dawn of a new era in galactic history.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/A_New_Dawn-SWP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20170110083833)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/A_New_Dawn-SWP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170110083833) 

The founding of the New Republic marked the dawn of a new era in galactic history.

 

Following the Battle of Endor, the Rebel Alliance transitioned into the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"). The Galactic Civil War reached a new crescendo as the New Republic made numerous advances on multiple fronts against the bewildered remnants of the Empire.[[106]](#cite_note-Aftermath-106) The Alliance and subsequent New Republic foiled [Operation: Cinder](/wiki/Operation:_Cinder "Operation: Cinder"), a posthumous contingency plan by the Emperor to devastate Naboo and at least a dozen other worlds.[[107]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_3-107)[[108]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_4-108) In the [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") after the events at Endor, New Republic and Imperial forces clashed on numerous fronts including the [Anoat sector](/wiki/Anoat_sector "Anoat sector"),[[26]](#cite_note-Uprising-26) Malastare, Geonosis, [Naalol](/wiki/Naalol "Naalol"), [Sevarcos](/wiki/Sevarcos "Sevarcos"), and [Akiva](/wiki/Akiva "Akiva").[[106]](#cite_note-Aftermath-106) A [civil war](/wiki/Coruscant_civil_war "Coruscant civil war") also broke out on the galactic capital of Coruscant.[[87]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-87)

By [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY "5 ABY"),[[109]](#cite_note-Life_Debt_date-109) the New Republic had reconstituted the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate") on [Chandrila](/wiki/Chandrila "Chandrila") and gained control of the HoloNet and large swaths of the galaxy, including Akiva and Kuat. Solo, Chewbacca, and a team of Wookiee [exiles](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") and other allies also [liberated](/wiki/Liberation_of_Kashyyyk "Liberation of Kashyyyk") Kashyyyk from Imperial rule. However, the chaos caused by the Civil War and the death of [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord") [Jabba Desilijic Tiure](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure") which occurred before Palpatine’s death allowed various criminal factions including the [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") lord [Eleodie Maracavanya](/wiki/Eleodie_Maracavanya "Eleodie Maracavanya") and the [Red Key Raiders](/wiki/Red_Key_Raiders "Red Key Raiders") to gain traction. A string of Imperial defeats led Grand Admiral [Rae Sloane](/wiki/Rae_Sloane "Rae Sloane") to propose [peace talks](/wiki/Imperial%E2%80%93Republic_peace_talks "Imperial–Republic peace talks") with [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(New_Republic) "Chancellor (New Republic)") Mon Mothma. However, the [attack](/wiki/Attack_on_Chandrila "Attack on Chandrila") on Chandrila destroyed the mood for diplomacy and enabled [Fleet Admiral](/wiki/Fleet_Admiral "Fleet Admiral") [Gallius Rax](/wiki/Gallius_Rax "Gallius Rax") to seize power.[[87]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-87)

 [![In the aftermath of the Battle of Jakku, the Galactic Empire formally capitulated to the New Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fc/Graveyard_of_the_Empire.png/revision/latest?cb=20171116043810) [![In the aftermath of the Battle of Jakku, the Galactic Empire formally capitulated to the New Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fc/Graveyard_of_the_Empire.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20171116043810)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fc/Graveyard_of_the_Empire.png/revision/latest?cb=20171116043810) 

In the aftermath of the Battle of Jakku, the Galactic Empire formally capitulated to the New Republic.

 

Proclaiming himself [Counselor to the Empire](/wiki/Counselor_to_the_Empire "Counselor to the Empire"), Rax brought most of the Imperial remnants to the desert world of [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku") for a [showdown](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku") with the New Republic. In truth, Rax planned to execute the final stage of Emperor Palpatine's [Contingency](/wiki/Contingency "Contingency") which involved exploding the planet Jakku in order to destroy what remained of the Empire. Rax planned to lead a worthy [remnant](/wiki/Unknown_Regions_Imperial_remnant "Unknown Regions Imperial remnant") into the Unknown Regions to build a new order. Several months later, New Republic agents discovered Rax's forces and the Senate dispatched a fleet to Jakku. Amidst the fighting, Sloane joined forces with New Republic Agents [Norra](/wiki/Norra_Wexley "Norra Wexley") and her son [Brentin Lore Wexley](/wiki/Brentin_Lore_Wexley "Brentin Lore Wexley") to foil Rax's plan. Meanwhile, Mas Amedda escaped house arrest and signed the [Galactic Concordance](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance") with Chancellor Mothma, facilitating the Empire's [surrender](/wiki/Imperial_Instruments_of_Surrender "Imperial Instruments of Surrender") to the New Republic. While the New Republic celebrated its victory, Sloane and other loyal Imperial forces fled into the Unknown Regions.[[31]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-31)

 [![Formed from a secret Imperial Contingency, the First Order of the Unknown Regions challenged the New Republic's place in the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/HuxAndStormtroopersAtCommandCenter-TFAOfficialTeaser.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150418182535) [![Formed from a secret Imperial Contingency, the First Order of the Unknown Regions challenged the New Republic's place in the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/HuxAndStormtroopersAtCommandCenter-TFAOfficialTeaser.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150418182535)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/HuxAndStormtroopersAtCommandCenter-TFAOfficialTeaser.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150418182535) 

Formed from a secret Imperial Contingency, the First Order of the Unknown Regions challenged the New Republic's place in the galaxy.

 

Following the Battle of Jakku, the defeated remnants of the Empire signed the Galactic Concordance, which imposed harsh war reparations and demilitarized the galaxy. With the Empire defeated, the New Republic turned its attention to reshaping the galactic order. Under New Republic rule, the galaxy endured peace for the next twenty-nine years. A group of Imperial hardliners eventually left Imperial space and rebuilt themselves upon joining the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order"), a military junta founded by former Imperials in the Unknown Regions secretly dedicated to overthrowing the Republic. In the veil of the Unknown Regions, the First Order rearmed their [military forces](/wiki/First_Order_military "First Order military") and built [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base") in anticipation for their war to retake the galaxy, though this was all in direct violation of the Galactic Concordance.[[28]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-28)

By [28 ABY](/wiki/28_ABY "28 ABY"),[[110]](#cite_note-Bloodline_date-110) the New Republic had become weakened by infighting between two powerful factions: the [Populists](/wiki/Populists "Populists"), who sought greater autonomy, and the [Centrists](/wiki/Centrists "Centrists"), who desired a stronger central government. The New Republic's inability to enforce financial regulations and patrol the galactic shipping lanes allowed criminal factions such as [Rinnrivin Di](/wiki/Rinnrivin_Di "Rinnrivin Di")'s [cartel](/wiki/Rinnrivin_Di%27s_cartel "Rinnrivin Di's cartel") and the [Amaxine warriors](/wiki/Amaxine_warriors_(New_Republic_Era) "Amaxine warriors (New Republic Era)") to [emerge](/wiki/Napkin_Bombing "Napkin Bombing"). In secret, these were front organizations that had been created by the First Order to generate revenue for its rearmament program and to subvert the New Republic. With the New Republic leadership unwilling to take action against the threat of the First Order to its existence, [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") founded a paramilitary outfit called the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance").[[111]](#cite_note-Bloodline-111)

### First Order-Resistance War[]

#### Rise of the First Order[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [First Order-Resistance War](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War")

:   "*Today is the end of the Republic! The end of a regime that acquiesces to disorder! At this very moment, in a system far from here the New Republic lies to the galaxy while secretly supporting the treachery of the loathsome Resistance. This fierce machine which you have built, upon which we stand, will bring an end to the Senate! To their cherished fleet! All remaining systems will bow to the First Order! And will remember this as the last day of the Republic!*"
:   ―Armitage Hux[[112]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-112)

 [![The completion of Starkiller Base provided the First Order with the power of destroying the New Republic in a single preemptive attack.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Hux_and_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425032958) [![The completion of Starkiller Base provided the First Order with the power of destroying the New Republic in a single preemptive attack.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Hux_and_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160425032958)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Hux_and_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425032958) 

The completion of Starkiller Base provided the First Order with the power of destroying the New Republic in a single preemptive attack.

 

During the Cold War, the [Borderlands](/wiki/Borderlands "Borderlands") had become a buffer zone between the New Republic and the expanding First Order. Unwilling to risk conflict with the Order, the Republic ordered its military to avoid hostilities with any of it forces.[[113]](#cite_note-BTA-113) After failing to stop Resistance [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") [BB-8](/wiki/BB-8 "BB-8"), [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), former [stormtrooper](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper") [Finn](/wiki/Finn "Finn"), Solo and Chewbacca from escaping with a [map](/wiki/Map_to_Skywalker "Map to Skywalker") leading to Luke, the last Jedi, who had gone into self-exile after his [efforts to restore the Jedi Order were destroyed](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple"), the First Order used their superweapon on Starkiller Base to launch a preemptive attack on the New Republic’s current capital Hosnian Prime[[112]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-112) in [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY").[[53]](#cite_note-Timelines-53) Marking the start of the [Starkiller crisis](/wiki/Starkiller_crisis "Starkiller crisis"), the [Hosnian Cataclysm](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm") was witnessed across the galaxy since the First Order had discovered a way of firing [dark energy](/wiki/Dark_energy "Dark energy") through [sub-hyperspace](/wiki/Sub-hyperspace "Sub-hyperspace") within [minutes](/wiki/Standard_minute "Standard minute").[[114]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-114) In response, the Resistance [destroyed](/wiki/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base "Battle of Starkiller Base") Starkiller Base.[[112]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-112)

Prior to the outbreak of the First Order-Resistance War, Resistance [spy](/wiki/Spy "Spy") [Kazuda Xiono](/wiki/Kazuda_Xiono "Kazuda Xiono") was posted to the *[Colossus](/wiki/Colossus "Colossus")*, a [supertanker fuel depot](/wiki/Supertanker_fuel_depot "Supertanker fuel depot") based on the Mid Rim planet [Castilon](/wiki/Castilon "Castilon").[[115]](#cite_note-The_Recruit-115) The *Colossus* was subsequently [occupied](/wiki/Occupation_of_the_Colossus "Occupation of the Colossus") by the First Order,[[116]](#cite_note-TFOO-116) which wanted to exploit the station as a military supply line.[[117]](#cite_note-The_New_Trooper-117) Following the Hosnian Cataclysm, Xiono and rebel veteran Commander [Jarek Yeager](/wiki/Jarek_Yeager "Jarek Yeager") led an [uprising](/wiki/Battle_of_Castilon "Battle of Castilon") and brought the *Colossus* into space.[[118]](#cite_note-No_Escape_Part_2-118) In response, the First Order launched a [hunt](/wiki/Hunt_for_the_Colossus "Hunt for the Colossus") for the *Colossus*, seeking to destroy it.[[119]](#cite_note-Into_the_Unknown-119)

 [![Kylo Ren, the grandson of Darth Vader, usurped Snoke's place as the Supreme Leader of the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DarkOrder.png/revision/latest?cb=20230401004411) [![Kylo Ren, the grandson of Darth Vader, usurped Snoke's place as the Supreme Leader of the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DarkOrder.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230401004411)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DarkOrder.png/revision/latest?cb=20230401004411) 

Kylo Ren, the grandson of Darth Vader, usurped Snoke's place as the Supreme Leader of the First Order.

 

Despite the destruction of Starkiller Base, the Hosnian Cataclysm decapitated the New Republic.
