As a result, [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke") deployed his [legions](/wiki/Legion "Legion") to seize military control over the galaxy. Rey predicted the major systems would fall to the First Order within weeks. The First Order also launched an offensive against the Resistance, [destroying](/wiki/Battle_of_D%27Qar "Battle of D'Qar") their base on D'Qar and [pursuing](/wiki/Battle_of_Oetchi "Battle of Oetchi") them through space with a [hyperspace tracker](/wiki/Hyperspace_tracker "Hyperspace tracker"). Though the First Order inflicted heavy casualties on the Resistance, the First Order sustained serious losses when [Vice Admiral](/wiki/Vice_Admiral "Vice Admiral") [Amilyn Holdo](/wiki/Amilyn_Holdo "Amilyn Holdo") [rammed](/wiki/Holdo_maneuver "Holdo maneuver") the Resistance's flagship the [*Raddus*](/wiki/Raddus_(MC85_Star_Cruiser) "Raddus (MC85 Star Cruiser)") into Supreme Leader Snoke's flagship the *[Supremacy](/wiki/Supremacy "Supremacy")* while he was assassinated by his apprentice and Anakin’s grandson [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), who claimed the title of Supreme Leader. Ren pursued the surviving members of the Resistance to the planet [Crait](/wiki/Crait "Crait"). There, Luke made his [last stand](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait") which gave the Resistance and Rey enough time to escape aboard the *Millennium Falcon*.[[120]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-120)

#### Rise of the galaxy[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Uprising against the First Order](/wiki/Uprising_against_the_First_Order "Uprising against the First Order")

:   "*People are rising up all over the galaxy. Poe, we did it.*"  
    "*We did it.*"
:   ―Finn and Poe Dameron — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/PeopleAreRising-TheRiseOfSkywalker.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250402194337)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:PeopleAreRising-TheRiseOfSkywalker.flac "File:PeopleAreRising-TheRiseOfSkywalker.flac"))[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-121)

 [![The Final Order was a Sith fleet constructed by the followers of Emperor Palpatine, who was resurrected on Exegol.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/59/Xyston-engines.png/revision/latest?cb=20211008042755) [![The Final Order was a Sith fleet constructed by the followers of Emperor Palpatine, who was resurrected on Exegol.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/59/Xyston-engines.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211008042755)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/59/Xyston-engines.png/revision/latest?cb=20211008042755) 

The Final Order was a Sith fleet constructed by the followers of Emperor Palpatine, who was resurrected on Exegol.

 

Although Emperor Palpatine's body was destroyed during the Battle of Endor, he [transferred](/wiki/Transference "Transference") his spirit into a clone after the fall of the Empire, however the process that created it was unfinished, forcing him to inhabit an unstable vessel and survived for another generation while his followers, a [Sith cult](/wiki/Sith_cult "Sith cult") known as the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal"), created the [Final Order](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order")—a massive armada of [*Xyston*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Xyston-class_Star_Destroyer "Xyston-class Star Destroyer") capable of destroying planets.[[56]](#cite_note-SOTS-56)

With the galaxy at war again and the Final Order complete, Palpatine came out of hiding and announced his return[[13]](#cite_note-TSWB-13) in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY").[[122]](#cite_note-IX_Date-122) In his [Broadcast](/wiki/Exegol_Broadcast "Exegol Broadcast") he demanded the submission of every world in the galaxy and revealed his true identity as a Sith Lord, which he no longer treated to be secret. The inhabitants of the galaxy were sent into a state of disbelief and fright when they learnt of Emperor Palpatine's survival.[[13]](#cite_note-TSWB-13) Kylo Ren, having vowed never to serve another master and believing in letting go of the past,[[35]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-35) regarded Palpatine as an intolerable threat to his power as Supreme Leader.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-121) As a result, Ren's priorities shifted from defeating the Resistance and suppressing their galaxy wide rebellion against his rule,[[35]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-35) to finding the Sith Lord so he could finish what his grandfather started and destroy the Sith once more.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-121)

 [![Ren tracked Palpatine to Exegol, where he discovered the Sith fleet as well as the secret of Rey's lineage.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/SidiousandKyloRen-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401232210) [![Ren tracked Palpatine to Exegol, where he discovered the Sith fleet as well as the secret of Rey's lineage.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/SidiousandKyloRen-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200401232210)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/SidiousandKyloRen-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401232210) 

Ren tracked Palpatine to Exegol, where he discovered the Sith fleet as well as the secret of Rey's lineage.

 

Using his grandfather’s [wayfinder](/wiki/Vader%27s_wayfinder "Vader's wayfinder") acquired on [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"), Ren journeyed to Exegol where he discovered Emperor Palpatine along with the Sith Eternal and the Final Order. He revealed his role behind the creation of Snoke and turning Ren to the dark side; he then offered the Sith fleet and title of Emperor to Ren if he killed Rey, the last Jedi before being warned that she was, in fact, his granddaughter.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-121)

With the help of the embittered General [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux"), the Resistance discovered Palpatine returned with a immense armada to attack the free worlds in sixteen hours and reinforce the First Order so he can rule the galaxy again and resurrect the Empire from its ashes to complete the final stages of the contingency of his master plan to achieve the Revenge of the Sith. Rey, Finn, Dameron, Chewbacca, BB-8, and C-3PO embarked on a mission to recover Palpatine’s [wayfinder](/wiki/Emperor%27s_wayfinder "Emperor's wayfinder") to reach Exegol. Following a series of adventures with the First Order and [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren"), Rey acquired a wayfinder and [fought](/wiki/Mission_to_Kef_Bir "Mission to Kef Bir") with Ren on [Kef Bir](/wiki/Kef_Bir "Kef Bir"), in the process discovering her true [lineage](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family") as Sidious' granddaughter. After sensing the death of his mother, and conversing with the spirit of his father, Ren returned to the [light side](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force") and reclaimed his identity as Ben.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-121)

 [![The planet Kijimi was destroyed as a demonstration of the Sith Eternal's power.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/KijimiGoBoom-TROS.png/revision/latest?cb=20230129061416) [![The planet Kijimi was destroyed as a demonstration of the Sith Eternal's power.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/KijimiGoBoom-TROS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230129061416)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/KijimiGoBoom-TROS.png/revision/latest?cb=20230129061416) 

The planet Kijimi was destroyed as a demonstration of the Sith Eternal's power.

 

Having sworn fealty to Palpatine once more like he did during the dark times of the Empire after Ben's renunciation of the dark side, [Allegiant General](/wiki/Allegiant_General "Allegiant General") [Enric Pryde](/wiki/Enric_Pryde "Enric Pryde") deployed the *[Derriphan](/wiki/Derriphan "Derriphan")*—one of the Star Destroyers from Exegol—to [Kijimi](/wiki/Kijimi "Kijimi"). The *Derriphan* used its [axial superlaser](/wiki/Axial_superlaser "Axial superlaser") to [destroy](/wiki/Destruction_of_Kijimi "Destruction of Kijimi") Kijimi, demonstrating the power of a single Star Destroyer of the Final Order after Pryde activated [Protocol 13](/wiki/Protocol_13 "Protocol 13"). Under the leadership of General Dameron and General Finn, the Resistance launched an attack on Exegol, attempting to prevent the Sith fleet's attack on the free worlds and union with the First Order.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-121)

Though initially outnumbered by the Sith Eternal's [forces](/wiki/Sith_Eternal_military "Sith Eternal military") during the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol"), the Resistance was reinforced by the [Citizens' Fleet](/wiki/Citizens%27_Fleet "Citizens' Fleet") led by General Calrissian. Meanwhile, Rey and Solo joined forces to defeat the Sith Lord for good at his [Sith Citadel](/wiki/Sith_Citadel "Sith Citadel") beneath Exegol. Realizing the two shared a [bond](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") as a [Force dyad](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad"), Palpatine drained their life energy and attacked the Resistance with [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning"). Rey was able to defeat Emperor Palpatine for good with the help of her Jedi predecessors, thereby preventing the return of the Sith. Despite succumbing to her injuries, Rey was resurrected by Solo, who [transferred](/wiki/Force_healing "Force healing") his life force to her at the cost of his life.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-121)

 [![The Citizens' Fleet joined the Resistance to defeat the Sith Eternal's forces during the Battle of Exegol.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/BattleofExegolcontinues-RiseIDW.png/revision/latest?cb=20221001190509) [![The Citizens' Fleet joined the Resistance to defeat the Sith Eternal's forces during the Battle of Exegol.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/BattleofExegolcontinues-RiseIDW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221001190509)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/BattleofExegolcontinues-RiseIDW.png/revision/latest?cb=20221001190509) 

The Citizens' Fleet joined the Resistance to defeat the Sith Eternal's forces during the Battle of Exegol.

 

The defeat of Palpatine and the Sith Eternal precipitated a galactic uprising against the First Order. As a result, the First Order's forces were beset by insurrection on various worlds, from [Bespin](/wiki/Uprising_on_Cloud_City "Uprising on Cloud City"), [Endor](/wiki/Uprising_on_Endor "Uprising on Endor"), and [Jakku](/wiki/Uprising_on_Jakku "Uprising on Jakku"),[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-121) to [Naboo](/wiki/Uprising_on_Naboo_(First_Order) "Uprising on Naboo (First Order)"), [Corellia](/wiki/Uprising_on_Corellia "Uprising on Corellia"), and [Coruscant](/wiki/Uprising_on_Coruscant "Uprising on Coruscant").[[123]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-123) The Resistance and the galaxy celebrated their victory[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-121) and the defeat of the First Order.[[13]](#cite_note-TSWB-13) In the wake of the conflict, the people of the galaxy began the long process of rebuilding their home after the destruction brought about by the First Order-Resistance War. Resistance historian Captain [Beaumont Kin](/wiki/Beaumont_Kin "Beaumont Kin") was given the task of overseeing an excavation of the Sith Citadel and wrote and published his new book *[The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire](/wiki/The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Galactic_Empire "The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire")* to educate the people about the Imperial regime. Rey, meanwhile, claimed the Skywalker name, became a Jedi Master like Luke did, and started to rebuild the Jedi Order to maintain peace and justice in the galaxy and balance in the Force.[[124]](#cite_note-Rise_and_Fall-124)

## Behind the scenes[]

 [![A slightly inaccurate map featuring several major regions as printed in ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/TheGalaxy-GEG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250714002212) [![A slightly inaccurate map featuring several major regions as printed in ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/TheGalaxy-GEG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250714002212)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/TheGalaxy-GEG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250714002212) 

A slightly inaccurate map featuring several major regions as printed in *[Star Wars: The Galactic Explorer's Guide](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Galactic_Explorer%27s_Guide "Star Wars: The Galactic Explorer's Guide")*

 

The galaxy first appeared in the [1977](/wiki/1977 "1977") film, [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope").[[46]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-46) In the [*Star Wars* Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") continuity, the galaxy was said to have 3.2 billion habitable systems.[[125]](#cite_note-EA-125) However, the [Canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") books *[Star Wars: The Visual Encyclopedia](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Visual_Encyclopedia "Star Wars: The Visual Encyclopedia")* and *[The Star Wars Book](/wiki/The_Star_Wars_Book "The Star Wars Book")* stated that the galaxy only had 3.2 million.[[1]](#cite_note-VE-1)[[13]](#cite_note-TSWB-13) This statistic was later corrected in later reprintings of *Star Wars: The Visual Encyclopedia*.[[1]](#cite_note-VE-1)

The 2025 reference book *[Star Wars: Complete Locations, New Edition](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Complete_Locations,_New_Edition "Star Wars: Complete Locations, New Edition")* utilized the [Standard Galactic Grid](/wiki/Standard_Galactic_Grid "Standard Galactic Grid") system in its map of the galaxy, directly copying the old system used in the 2009 legends reference book *[The Essential Atlas](/wiki/The_Essential_Atlas "The Essential Atlas")*. Both books labeled each grid as being 5,000 light-years in diameter with 21 grids vertically and 23 grids horizontally overlaid on a map of the galaxy, meaning the galaxy is approximately 105,000 light-years on the y-axis and 115,000 light-years on the x-axis.[[126]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Complete_Locations,_New_Edition-126)[[125]](#cite_note-EA-125)

[↑](#cite_ref-SG_3-0) *[Star Wars Super Graphic: A Visual Guide to a Galaxy Far, Far Away](/wiki/Star_Wars_Super_Graphic:_A_Visual_Guide_to_a_Galaxy_Far,_Far_Away "Star Wars Super Graphic: A Visual Guide to a Galaxy Far, Far Away")* 4. ↑ [4.0](#cite_ref-Altaya_4-0) [4.1](#cite_ref-Altaya_4-1) "[*Millennium Falcon*](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon_(reference_book) "Millennium Falcon (reference book)")" — *[Star Wars Encyclopedia](/wiki/Star_Wars_Encyclopedia_(series) "Star Wars Encyclopedia (series)")* 5. ↑ [5.0](#cite_ref-CE25_light-year_note_5-0) [5.1](#cite_ref-CE25_light-year_note_5-1) The reference book, *[Star Wars: Complete Locations, New Edition](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Complete_Locations,_New_Edition "Star Wars: Complete Locations, New Edition")* and [*Star Wars* Galaxy Map](/wiki/Star_Wars_Galaxy_Map "Star Wars Galaxy Map") article on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") utilize the [Standard Galactic Grid](/wiki/Standard_Galactic_Grid "Standard Galactic Grid") in their maps of the galaxy, denoting a single grid square as being equivalent to 5,000 [light-years](/wiki/Light-year "Light-year"). There are 21 grids vertically and 23 grids horizontally overlaid on the maps of the galaxy, therefore the size of the galaxy can be determined to be approximately 105,000 light-years on the y-axis and 115,000 light-years on the x-axis. 6. ↑ [6.0](#cite_ref-Catalyst_6-0) [6.1](#cite_ref-Catalyst_6-1) *[Catalyst: A Rogue One Novel](/wiki/Catalyst:_A_Rogue_One_Novel "Catalyst: A Rogue One Novel")* 7. [↑](#cite_ref-Old_Galactic_Republic_42-0) *[Thrawn Ascendancy: Chaos Rising](/wiki/Thrawn_Ascendancy:_Chaos_Rising "Thrawn Ascendancy: Chaos Rising")* states that the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") fought against the [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire"). As the Empire was destroyed by the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the modern Republic's founding per *[Star Wars Propaganda: A History of Persuasive Art in the Galaxy](/wiki/Star_Wars_Propaganda:_A_History_of_Persuasive_Art_in_the_Galaxy "Star Wars Propaganda: A History of Persuasive Art in the Galaxy")*, and the Republic that existed prior to the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith")'s fall is referred to as the Old Republic by *Star Wars Propaganda*, it can be found that the Old Republic was the Galactic Republic, only that the government of the time before the Sith's fall came to be commonly known as the Old Republic. 43. ↑ [43.0](#cite_ref-25,000_BBY_Date_Note_43-0) [43.1](#cite_ref-25,000_BBY_Date_Note_43-1) *[The Star Wars Book](/wiki/The_Star_Wars_Book "The Star Wars Book")* places the founding of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") and the [Old Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") to around 25,000 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), which corresponds to [25,000 BBY](/wiki/25,000_BBY "25,000 BBY") per *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*. Therefore, they must have been founded around 25,000 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). 44. ↑ [44.0](#cite_ref-Rising_Storm_44-0) [44.1](#cite_ref-Rising_Storm_44-1) [44.2](#cite_ref-Rising_Storm_44-2) [44.3](#cite_ref-Rising_Storm_44-3) *[The High Republic: The Rising Storm](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_The_Rising_Storm "The High Republic: The Rising Storm")* 45. [↑](#cite_ref-Mandalorian_super_commando_61-0) [StarWars.com Encyclopedia](/wiki/Encyclopedia_(StarWars.com) "StarWars.com Encyclopedia") [Mandalorian super commando](https://web.archive.org/web/20130210110425/http://starwars.com/explore/encyclopedia/groups/mandalorian-super-commando) in the [Encyclopedia](/wiki/Encyclopedia_(StarWars.com) "Encyclopedia (StarWars.com)") ([original site](http://starwars.com/explore/encyclopedia/groups/mandalorian-super-commando) is defunct) 62. [↑](#cite_ref-Galactic_Republic_Date_Note_62-0) *[The Star Wars Book](/wiki/The_Star_Wars_Book "The Star Wars Book")* dates the restoration of the Republic to 1,032 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), which corresponds to [1032 BBY](/wiki/1032_BBY "1032 BBY") per *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*. Therefore, the restoration must have occurred in 1032 BBY. 63. [↑](#cite_ref-Yavin_Code_Date_Note_63-0) *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates the events of "[The Big Bang](/wiki/The_Big_Bang "The Big Bang")" to [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"). In the episode, it is stated that the Yavin Code is about a [thousand years](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") old. Therefore, the Code must have been established about a millennium prior to 19 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). 64. [↑](#cite_ref-The_Big_Bang_64-0) [TCW mini logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars") *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* — "[The Big Bang](/wiki/The_Big_Bang "The Big Bang")" 65. ↑ [65.0](#cite_ref-EotS1_65-0) [65.1](#cite_ref-EotS1_65-1) [65.2](#cite_ref-EotS1_65-2) [65.3](#cite_ref-EotS1_65-3) [65.4](#cite_ref-EotS1_65-4) [*The High Republic: Eye of the Storm* 1](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Eye_of_the_Storm_1 "The High Republic: Eye of the Storm 1") 66. ↑ [66.0](#cite_ref-Light_of_the_Jedi_66-0) [66.1](#cite_ref-Light_of_the_Jedi_66-1) *[The High Republic: Light of the Jedi](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Light_of_the_Jedi "The High Republic: Light of the Jedi")* 67. ↑ [67.0](#cite_ref-Path_Ven_67-0) [67.1](#cite_ref-Path_Ven_67-1) [67.2](#cite_ref-Path_Ven_67-2) [67.3](#cite_ref-Path_Ven_67-3) [67.4](#cite_ref-Path_Ven_67-4) [67.5](#cite_ref-Path_Ven_67-5) *[The High Republic: Path of Vengeance](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Path_of_Vengeance "The High Republic: Path of Vengeance")* 68. ↑ [68.0](#cite_ref-Temptation_68-0) [68.1](#cite_ref-Temptation_68-1) [68.2](#cite_ref-Temptation_68-2) [68.3](#cite_ref-Temptation_68-3) *[The High Republic: Temptation of the Force](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Temptation_of_the_Force "The High Republic: Temptation of the Force")* 69. ↑ [69.0](#cite_ref-EotS2_69-0) [69.1](#cite_ref-EotS2_69-1) [*The High Republic: Eye of the Storm* 2](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Eye_of_the_Storm_2 "The High Republic: Eye of the Storm 2") 70. ↑ [70.0](#cite_ref-TOTJ_Choices_70-0) [70.1](#cite_ref-TOTJ_Choices_70-1) [Tales of the Jedi logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Jedi_(television_series) "Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi (television series)") *[Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Jedi_(television_series) "Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi (television series)")* — "[Choices](/wiki/Choices "Choices")" 71. [↑](#cite_ref-CIS_Formation_Date_Note_74-0) *[Rise of the Separatists](/wiki/Rise_of_the_Separatists "Rise of the Separatists")* establishes that the [Raxus Address](/wiki/Raxus_Address "Raxus Address") and following foundation of the Confederacy of Independent Systems occurred two [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"), which, along with the other events of [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones"), *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates to [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"). Therefore, simple math can be used to find the CIS was formed in [24 BBY](/wiki/24_BBY "24 BBY"). Additionally, because the ratification of the [Geonosian accord](/wiki/Geonosian_accord "Geonosian accord") first appeared in *Attack of the Clones*, the events of which are dated to 22 BBY by *Galactic Atlas*, the accord must have been ratified in 22 BBY. 75.
